I tried to collect best paper awards from the top-tier conferences in each area, but some conferences do not have such an award (e.g. SIGGRAPH, CAV). "Distinguished paper award" and "outstanding paper award" are included but not "best student paper" (e.g. NIPS) or "best 10-year old paper" (e.g. POPL)</p><br><table><thead><td colspan=3><a name="aaai">AAAI (Artificial Intelligence)</a></td></thead><tr><td rowspan=2><b>2013</b></td><td><a href="http://scholar.google.com/scholar?as_q=&num=10&btnG=Search+Scholar&as_epq=HC-Search:+Learning+Heuristics+and+Cost+Functions+for+Structured+Prediction&as_oq=&as_eq=&as_occt=any&as_sauthors=Doppa">HC-Search: Learning Heuristics and Cost Functions for Structured Prediction</a></td><td>Janardhan Rao Doppa, Oregon State University<a href="#" onclick="this.nextSibling.style.display = 'block';
